                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Boundary Lines
Everyone, when you think of 'boundary lines,' American citizens might think of the Canadian border and the Mexican border. Within the United States, there are boundary lines centered around each state, between states. Also, within those states, if you look at organizations or individuals, they are all surrounded by boundary lines. Broadly speaking, there are boundary lines centered around North and South America, and there are boundary lines in Asia; everything is surrounded by boundary lines. 
Everyone has boundary lines.
So, why are there boundary lines? The reason there are boundary lines is that the owners are different. In the area that is occupied, the position is different, and the owner is different. Furthermore, these boundary lines serve as a protective right, a protective right to prevent external invasions.
You are here today, and our Unification Church may seem to have nothing, but when it comes to whether there are boundary lines or not, you might say there are none, but that is not true. There are indeed boundary lines. There are also lines that should not be crossed, lines that say do not cross. If you cross that line, you will inevitably be determined to belong to something else in some other form.
Nowadays, when we look at this earth, we hear terms like the democratic world and the communist world. The boundary lines of the United States, the boundary lines of the democratic world are clearly drawn. If you were to split this world in half, you could say this is the democratic world, and this is the communist world, but the democratic world is just a continuous line. However, how is the communist world structured? It is like this, going around in a circle. (He illustrates while speaking)
Therefore, if the boundary lines are like this... we see a straight line drawn here, indicating a boundary line going like this. As it goes, it expands. It keeps expanding and widening. This is what we need to think about.
Now, if we look at it this way, it means that there has been a historical battle centered around Satan and God. In that process, they are fighting centered around the form of religion, and religion itself has become a boundary line. So, what about the Unification Church? Does the Unification Church have a boundary line between Satan and God, or not? "It does." That boundary line is at the highest point, where it is clearly divided. (He illustrates while speaking)
When we look at religion, it rises from primitive religions to higher religions. At the very top, is there a boundary line or not? "There is." What does that mean? It means that God also has a boundary line. God is omniscient and omnipotent, so there is nothing He cannot do. However, there are limits that God should not cross. If God were to cross a certain boundary line, something would happen that should not happen.
If He were to cross it, He would have to present conditions beyond the content that could defend that boundary line. If He crosses without doing so, He falls under the conditions. Presenting defensive conditions to cross that line is harder than not crossing it at all. Therefore, He must not cross it. No matter how well prepared, there is a risk involved.
9
What boundary lines do you have?
Everyone, when God said to Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden, "Do not eat," what is that? It is a boundary net. If you do not think of that boundary line as a boundary line and forget that you must protect yourself, and just think as you usually do, problems will arise. What about the teacher? The teacher is the same.
When we look at it this way, you might think, "The world is on God's side, and the evil world is on Satan's side," but you need to think about what the boundary line is among you. We have five senses, and if the eyes see this way, the thoughts go that way, and everything is in conflict. It is all like that, isn’t it?
Now, if you think about military aspects, what is a stronghold? Generally, when you look at the army, they look for a triangular area. They look for a place that is narrow and shaped like this. So, if the eyes can see this way, and if the eyes are like this, then it means there are cannons placed on the eyelids. If the eyes see this way, it means they are guarding with cannons above and below the eyes. (He expresses this through actions) Satan is guarding like this. If your thoughts and heart are like that, then what happens if the heart goes elsewhere? So, is it better to have long boundary lines or short ones? "Short ones." Why? Why is that? In the end, having long boundary lines means there are many places that can be attacked and invaded. If it is long, that is the case. So, it is dangerous.
When you look at some people, they think differently, see differently, and then act differently; such people have long boundary lines. They are confused people, confused people. It should be a straight line, but some people are like this, and there are people like this. (He illustrates while speaking) There are all kinds of people. (Laughter) Some people can turn around several times a day. They can be upside down and go back and forth like this. Therefore, you have to think about what kind of boundary line you have. (He laughs)
It is like dragging that around. You drag it around your whole life. So, the question is, what kind of boundary line do you have? The boundary line is the issue, the boundary line. Think about it.
The most dangerous thing among our boundary lines
So, what is the most dangerous thing among our boundary lines? It is the tendency to take side paths. So, what does that mean in our lives? Let’s take a moment to consider. We can divide it into external and internal. Externally, what is needed in relative relationships? Let’s consider that. What is it? Money, money can be one. Then knowledge, that is knowledge. And what else? Power, power. Generally, we grasp these things. Money pulls me in.
So, what is it that draws me in? What are the conditions under which I can be tempted? That is my internal issue. That is precisely greed, greed. What kind of greed is it? This greed is bad. It is greed for myself.
Boundary line expansion issue
If you have desires, centered around those desires... (He illustrates while speaking) If there are such desires, and you are standing here, a person who only thinks of themselves is like this, crossing the boundary line quickly. This is how they live. There are people like this. Personal desires lead to this. If you make a small mistake, it is dangerous.
So, how do you expand that boundary line? I am in the middle, and there are desires wearing hats like family, tribe, nation, and state. For the sake of the family... They are wearing these big things and drawing desires. In that case, the boundary line expands from here. Wouldn’t you want to draw such a boundary line? Ultimately, what does that mean? It means that the boundary line can be expanded. So, what happens? Because of me, the boundary line widens like this. Then, if someone tries to invade that person, the nation protects them, and the whole protects them. They cannot enter... That is similar to expanding the boundary line.
Because of this content, even if you did not know what it was today, because of this boundary line movement, the public is protected by the nation and the world, and the private is disliked by the nation, disliked by the family, and disliked by everyone. This conclusion is a valid conclusion. Because the flow of history has been like this, whether in the West or the East, throughout the historical process where people have established moral ethics, it has always been, "Be a public person. Be a person who keeps the law." There has never been a law that says, "Oh, do as you please." They did not teach that, and it is a fact that they have not gone through such a historical process. Does that seem likely? "Yes."
Therefore, this is what the public is, and this is what the private is, and it will resonate in your ears. So, what kind of people are you? If you have public desires, that is good the more you think about it. Public thoughts are good no matter how much you have. This is the same for God. When viewed centered around God, the claims that God makes are the boundary lines.
This is an undeniable fact.
12   Boundary Lines
So, what kind of advocate is God? Is He an American-style advocate? Is He an advocate like American citizens? "No." Then what kind of advocate is He? "He is a God-centered advocate." Well, how does that differ? Then let me ask you something. Is Americanism bigger or Godism bigger? "Godism." (He laughs) You know that. Godism is bigger.
What kind of advocacy is Godism? It is the advocacy of the whole, the whole. What is Americanism? It is a part, a partial advocacy. It is an advocacy that dislikes black people centered around white people. That is it. It is biased.
And there are many boundary lines even within America. German boundary lines, Jewish boundary lines, black boundary lines, white boundary lines... Right? "Yes." Godism says, "Throw all that away! What is this!" and discards everything. Do American people like that? "They like it." (Laughter) "They do not like it." People who will go to heaven are those who follow Godism, not Americanism. "Godism." Then can American people go to heaven or not? "No." (Laughter) They cannot go. When you look at it this way, the more boundary lines you have, the more likely you will go to the worst hell, and the fewer boundary lines you have, the more likely you will ascend to heaven. There will be a gradient of differences. Theoretically, that is the case.
From that perspective, you can immediately discover who will go to heaven and who will go to hell. Do you understand? It depends on what kind of person you like. Rather than someone who just blocks entry, you prefer someone who opens the door, who allows you to come at night or during the day, who lets you ride on top or push in. Such people have no boundary lines. So, do you prefer people with many boundary lines or people with no boundary lines? "No boundary lines." So, everyone prefers people with no boundary lines? "Yes."
What kind of advocate will you be? Will you be a God-centered advocate or an American advocate, or a black-centered advocate? "A God-centered advocate." You have many desires. Earlier, I said that personal desires are not good, but you have learned this. Desires for the world, public desires for the whole are good; those desires are good. You have understood this. Right? "Yes." That is right. Good. Now you know.
Now, you can immediately find out what kind of religion is like Godism among religions, and among nations and ideologies, we can immediately examine what is like Godism. If you only know this principle, you can draw boundary lines and judge and examine as much as you want.
The true ideology and true religion from the perspective of boundary lines
When comparing communism and democracy... which one is closer to God? Communism claims to advocate for workers and farmers while asserting dictatorial sovereignty. However, when you look at democracy, it does not think that way. It accepts both wealthy people and conscientious people, and farmers; it accepts everyone. When you look at people living in communist countries, even in East Germany, when they put up boundary lines, communists all went there thinking it was good, but they keep crossing over. Therefore, a person who stands in a position to draw boundary lines is bad.
When you look at it this way, the democratic world is closer to God than the communist world. What do communists do? They try to eliminate the bourgeois class completely. They do not think of saving them; they think of eliminating them. They do not think of assimilating them. They are all about punishment. Do you understand that? "Yes." Communism says, "Religion is the opium of the people." It is total annihilation, total annihilation. The Soviet Union now maintains a form of church for operational purposes. All of that is fake under the leadership of the Communist Party. It is formalistic. It is a camouflage strategy. They are not recognizing that religion exists; they are saying, "Prioritize what the Communist Party wants over the Bible. Then serve God." What is that boundary line? It is under Satan's authority, under Satan's authority.
From this perspective, religion has a specific boundary line. What is the boundary line of that religion? It is cosmopolitanism. Therefore, because people have a desire for something great and demand the whole, as long as they know the path of religion, everyone enters there. Throughout history, the saints who have taught have all followed that realm, and those people have become representatives who lead history because they are trying to follow an ideology closer to Godism. Therefore, in the end, the world cannot help but be encompassed within it.
14   Boundary Lines
When it comes to saints, what kind of people are they? Are they nationalists, or are they cosmopolitans? The greater the saint, the more they are globalists and universalists. When you look at the boundary lines of democracy and communism, you have understood which is better.
The same logic applies when looking at religions. What is the true religion? If there is a religion that cries out for a greater ideology than cosmopolitanism and Godism, it even encompasses God. It means that while seeking God, God enters into it. You just have to grasp it. (Laughter) Is that right or not? "It is right." Then is the Unification Church a religion or not? "It is a religion." Others now call it a sect or a cult.
You all oppose everything, don't you? What is religion? What kind of religion is the Unification Church? 
Does the world call it a religion? "Yes." Then what kind of religion is it? "Godism...." It's trying to follow Godism. It's a kind of Godism that aims to establish a greater principle than Godism. 
If you love, you transcend boundaries. 
Have you heard of God's heartism? (laughter) That's what it is. God alone cannot manifest heartism. There must be a counterpart to the heart. Heartism means I do what God wants, I do it.... Is that really true? "Yes." Then you thought God was high, but are you higher? (laughter) Isn't that right? Therefore, to fulfill God's heartism, you must say, "You are like me. I cannot be without you." You must be able to say that. Isn't that wonderful? Don't you want that? "Yes." This assertion has only been made by the Unification Church throughout history. If we put that in relative terms, it is cosmology. It was labeled that way because there were no letters to describe it.
Now, can you become someone who knows God? If you greet someone with "Good morning," would God also say "Good morning"? Do you want to be someone who loves God? (laughter) What kind of person do you want to be? You don't even need "Good morning." Just as soon as you see each other.... There are no boundaries. There is no greeting or anything. You just hold each other and love. (demonstrating with actions) There are no boundaries. Then, would you say that's wrong? Among those who love, "Oh, is there a rule that you don't greet each other? Men and women.... They are all different counterparts. There are all kinds of face-saving and laws." Is that so? (laughter) All boundaries are erased there.
Therefore, you must understand that there is no law condemning love. Love has no boundaries of law and transcends all boundaries. That is where this saying comes from. Is that right? Think about it. "That's right."
No matter how scary the law is in America and how they try to drive Reverend Moon out today, when you say you love America, you must accept it. When you understand that, the U.S. State Department should send a top 747 jumbo jet to take me. Can that happen? "Yes, it can." Really? (laughter) Does immigration law apply then? All laws, such as the Ministry of Justice and the Tax Office, collapse. Is that right or not? "That's right." Think seriously about it. Think coldly about it. Is that true? Is it really true? "Yes." Is that a fact or not? Is it certain? "Yes." No matter how fierce a lion-like person is, if you love that person and love their children, the boundaries of that household disappear when you love. It's the same.
What God loves the most is love.
So, what about hell? Do you think the boundaries of hell will remain in front of the two characters of love? Jesus died on the cross and preached in hell for three days. There, Satan said, "Hey, hey, you came in well, Jesus. Now you can't get out." Did he say that? Jesus knew this. That's why he said to love even your enemies. Hell is where enemies go, but in front of Jesus, who says he will love even there, hell's boundaries are abolished. Even if there are boundaries in heaven, can God stop someone who loves God and loves heaven? When you go to God's side, can He say, "Hey, hey, come greet me. Bring a gift. Bring a bribe"? Can He do that? "No, He cannot."
So, what is the best thing in this universe? "Love." What kind of love? "Love for others." Is it a love that only loves your own kind, regardless of how the world is or how others are? "Americans are good, but I don't like Germans, and I don't like Asians, and I don't like Reverend Moon." Is that the kind of love? That's why there are various kinds of love belonging to different principles, but what is the best? It is love belonging to Godism. That alone is the highest, and that conclusion comes out.
If you have that love, there are no boundaries in any family. If this world is evil and blocks that love because it doesn't know, it becomes a debt not only for the past and present but also for the future generations of that country. Why? Because this is a love that can move throughout all of history, from before history to after history, without boundaries. That love existed before history and will exist after history. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."
What does God like? What does the absolute omnipotent God like? It is neither the power He has nor the knowledge. Even if God were to give up everything, He would still want to hold onto this. Why? Because if He has this, the entire universe becomes His. Do you think that could be true? "Yes." There are no boundaries there. There are no boundaries. Therefore, it ultimately transcends distance. It transcends time and space. If the person you love is in England and you are in Korea, do you fall under the control of distance? "No, you don't." Right? "Yes." When you look at it this way, we didn't know this amazing thing. Did you know? 
So, what will you choose? What do you want to have? "Love." What kind of love? "Absolute love." Where can you find that? In established churches, in established churches? You are sitting here without even chairs; what is this? Why are you sitting here without a church? Why are you sitting here from early morning, getting cold? 
Women shouldn't sit in cold places; it's not good. That means you shouldn't come when it's cold. It's okay not to come. "No." Why "no"? What is "no"? Why? Why? It's simple. It's to find a connection that can relate to a higher love. That's why that conclusion comes out. 
We are people who follow heartism.
Even if you don't want to see the teacher, the teacher's words are wonderful, and when you hear such words, you feel inexplicably broadened and drawn closer. That's why you can't help but come. (applause) During such times, you go to God's threshold, to God's breath without boundaries. So you come at dawn.... Some people come and sit from two o'clock, shivering. (imitating shivering) Is that reasonable? "Yes, it is." You are not doing a losing business because you are weak. Some people come here, and when the teacher's saliva splatters, they think, "Oh, this is good." There are people like that. (laughter, applause) Why does such an extreme opposite phenomenon occur? Because there is love. Is that right? "Yes."
When you see that, think about how much the teacher has thought. I am a smart person. Think about how much the teacher has thought throughout his life. If there were a better way somewhere else, I would have gone there already. I would have already gone. I know communism well. If that were a good way, I would have become a communist. If the democracy that America advocates were good, I would have become someone welcomed in the democratic world, not someone opposed. No matter how much communism curses and how bad democracy is said to be, I know that this is the best, and I know that following the world of cosmological heart is the greatest path, so I am sacrificing my life and everything for this path. What kind of principle is that? It is God's heartism. That is why it can become one with God.
Although it seems that there are many boundaries in God's world and the earthly world, we don't know that; if we know, all will be abolished. Then, I will also say that I will liberate even the satanic world. I am saying we should liberate hell. There is an idealism in the world.... This is the last principle, the last principle. You must understand that this is the first principle that appears and the last principle. Whether that is true or not, the teacher's words are correct, right? Will you acknowledge that? "Yes."
Therefore, if you carry this heart, your victory is a predetermined principle. No matter where you are, even if you are crowded and imprisoned, when you come out, you will receive compensation thousands or tens of thousands of times. It won't take long before you are recognized by the king of that country, the president, and all the people.... Do you think that could happen? Is that possible? "Yes." It is a fact.
Love grows the more you do it.
Now that you know that.... Therefore, it is established here that only this wonderful love can govern the universe. God can also be governed by it. When you encounter this love, no matter how complicated and difficult the problems of today's world are, you can solve them, create one, and unify them. 
This may seem like a simple statement, but after an hour, if you truly understand this.... After hearing this, have your boundaries widened or narrowed? "Narrowed." In the past, a white girl would say, "Oh, I don't like black people," but as you hear this, it gradually becomes smaller. (laughter) You must see that this is more powerful than America's atomic bomb and stronger than any sovereign's authority.
When you see that, a great revolution is happening within this time frame. You don't know that fact. Think about it. This is something that can happen worldwide.... This is not a possibility; there is absoluteness here. We, who have this content, do not know it, but once we do, the world will become one. Is it better for the world to become one quickly or slowly? "Quickly." Why? Why? Because the more you use love, the more it disappears, right? "No." Love grows the more you do it. That's why it grows....
Look. When you love, you receive great love from God, but you also receive great love from the person you love. So how many times is this a business? More than twice. It's a multiple business. That's why love is a multidimensional business. It multiplies dimensionally. No matter how good money is, once you give it, it disappears. No matter how good knowledge is, the more you use it, the more it is consumed. All power is consumed the more you use it. Boundaries keep forming. Therefore, love sacrifices money, sacrifices power, sacrifices knowledge.... Can you exchange those for this love? The conclusion is that you cannot.
Become someone who cares for the world.
Now that you understand that well, will you just sit still? "No." What will you do? You are told to do love business, love business. White people should not only love white people but also love black people, and even reach out to Asia, to hell, anywhere. When this love is spread throughout the universe, will the people receiving that love be crying or happy? When I carry that love, the universe is drawn to me. Even if you tell it not to come, it comes. That is a fact.
Why did you come here at dawn? Do you like Reverend Moon? "Yes." I can't believe it. I can't believe it. "Please believe me." What you should believe is that it is better than Americanism, better than communism or democracy, and better than ordinary established churchism. That is why you must love even more. Now, when you eat, who do you eat for? "For God." Then if you are for God, do you just leave God alone while eating? You must do it like God. 
You must do it like God. Will you do that? Will you do that? "Yes." Oh, then, is it a big deal? "Yes."
To do that, do you like fundraising? "Yes." Why, why, why, why? Because you want to give to the world, you earn the hardest to give to the world.... Have you ever heard someone say, "Oh, welcome, come on in," when fundraising? "Yes." Really? What is that?
Are there more people who give out of joy or those who give because they have to? (laughter) There are many who give out of necessity, who are scorned, pointed at, humiliated, sometimes kicked, and spat upon, yet they earn not for themselves but for the world, for God. That is frightening. That is amazing. The price may be small, but it is worth thousands or tens of thousands of times.... Can that be true? "Yes." The teacher is the same. Even if everyone in America opposes, even if your parents oppose, he doesn't say, "Your parents oppose? That son of a gun." The more they oppose, the more he thinks without such thoughts, raising you to be a person for America, a person for the world. No matter how much the Unification Church is opposed....
Even though your parents generally oppose, he doesn't think, "I must make that enemy's child bad." He opposes. Rather, he is making you able to become an adult. Victory and defeat have already been decided. Who has won? You fight on the teacher's side, not on your parents' side against the teacher. How revolutionary is this? How great is this? You may oppose your parents by siding with the teacher, but you don't oppose the teacher by siding with your parents. Why? Because it is the truth. Is that right? "Yes." Why is that? Because you know it yourself. You know how shameful it is in your life, how shameful it is for your lineage, so you cannot defend it.
Only through love can we break down boundaries and create one world.
Are the people in the room? "It's San Francisco." Then where did the family here go? How many hours did it take to come here? Did it take about seven or eight hours? And did you come by bus? "Yes." Did it take about ten hours? "Yes." I see.

When a man and a woman completely unite, heaven and earth take notice, and God takes notice too. When you came here, you might have wondered, "What kind of person is the teacher?" But the teacher is just this kind of person. There's nothing special about it. There are two eyes, two nostrils, two ears, and one mouth. Some people think that when Jesus goes up to the second floor, he goes up without passing through the door, and when he comes down, he flies down, and that he eats without using a fork, just like this. (Laughter) That's not interesting.

Human beings themselves are nature. You must understand that perfect nature is sacred. You are the same. If you are not in accordance with the original nature that God created, then that is a problem. If it were in accordance with nature, it would be holy. Therefore, it is natural and holy for a person to eat with their hands raised, to blink their eyes while looking, and to engage in all these activities.

December 10, 1976 (Friday), Pasadena House (Los Angeles, USA).
* This message was given to blessed families in Japan, and the title was added by the editor.

So, is it holy for Jesus to live alone, or is it holy for him to live in marriage? Which is more holy? "Living in marriage." In order for you to become completely holy, it is necessary for two people to become perfect rather than just one person. That is more difficult.

Our Japanese family members might have thought that they could complete themselves while being alone, but after getting married, is it easier or harder to complete? Why are you not answering? Is it easier or harder? Which is it? "It’s difficult." How difficult? It is as difficult for a man and a woman to become one as it is for heaven and earth to become one. That is why if a perfect man and a perfect woman can completely unite, heaven and earth will all take notice, and God will take notice too. God is also concerned about that, which is why He pays attention.

You have learned the principle, but how much did God hope for the day Adam and Eve would be completed? Did He hope for it because it was easy, or because it was difficult? You have two eyes, and one eye looks this way while the other looks that way, right? You look this way and that way.

You come to America and train for three years, and then you return to Japan. After training in America, if the man is like the right eye and the woman is like the left eye, and one looks this way while the other looks that way, what will happen? (Laughter) Do you like people with crooked lower lips? Do you like people who limp? Really? "No." In the same way, when a man and a woman become one, and based on that united couple, their children become one, it is a cosmic event.

The most precious thing for a person is to create a family overflowing with love. 

You know, in America, there are countless families... When I cross over the mountains of Los Angeles, the boundary is very clear. I cross over the desert area and enter the green area, and as the flat land unfolds with many houses, I wonder, "Is that house really a happy house?" I thought there wouldn’t be many happy houses. As I mentioned, are there houses in America where there are father and mother, grandparents, and children living together, where three generations can live together? Raise your hand if you think there is a friend among those you know who lives like that. How is it? Is there? "No." Where did this sickness originate? Ultimately, it originated from one man and one woman.

Why are your grandparents and parents like that? They have inherited the tradition of their grandparents and have become that way. Because those grandparents lived that way and educated them that way, they have become like that.

If those grandparents had become the perfect ideal couple and played a role in making their parents an ideal couple, then the parents of that family would also strive to make their children ideal sons and daughters. Where is the most central place for a person to strive? It is not in society, nor in accumulating wealth, nor in personal success. The conclusion is that the most precious thing is to put the most effort and sincerity into the family. Have you thought about that? "Yes." But you probably thought about it in an American way, right?

You see, American young people think that once they turn 18, they are free and have nothing to do with their parents. Then what happens? As they get older, their interest in family should deepen, and their concern for their parents should grow thicker, yet once they turn 18, they lose interest in their parents and leave altogether.

Are there any young people among you who are interested in their grandparents? You may have some interest. But do you truly love them? Have you ever thought, "Even if I live alone for my whole life, I will make my grandparents happy"? No, you haven’t.

And what about your parents? There may be people who think about their parents. There are those who would devote their lives to doing something for their parents, but that happens when the parents have become one as a father and mother who can devote their lives. Would you want to do that even if you cannot be a good example for your children? You cannot do that.

If it were ideal... which parents would you want: those who devote their lives for their children, or those who divorce and abandon their children for their own satisfaction? Which parents do you prefer? "The first." Why? You need to understand that the reason you demand that is because there is a sincere appeal within you that you can also devote your life for your parents.

Therefore, if parents truly loved like that, even if they were to drive their children away, they would want to live in the back room, and no matter how difficult it is, they would want to be with those parents. You must understand that the emotional bond grows larger as parents sacrifice themselves. Do you think so? "Yes." It all becomes like that. Ultimately, if grandparents, anyone can sacrifice themselves for you, then according to that education, the sincere heart will respond, and the body will respond, and you cannot help but care for and respect them. We have learned that such origins arise here. Right? "Yes."

It is the same in the relationship between men and women, in the relationship between couples. Do you want a loving wife and a loving husband, or do you want a wife and husband who love for a while and then stop? Which do you want? "The first." Common Responsibility  
Everyone, this is Los Angeles, which is said to be the central city of the western United States. Seeing your faces, I see that you are all in your 20s, which makes me think back to that time for a moment. When I see young people, looking into their eyes, I think, "Wow, they are so vibrant," but older people are different. Times are different. (laughter)  
We are people who have chosen the inner world, unlike ordinary people.  
Looking at myself, I am over 50 years old, so it’s time that I should not act like I did in my youth, and I have realized that there are many things I should not do. (laughter) And now, wherever I go in America, everyone knows me. Because everyone is paying attention to me, I feel that it has become difficult to have an environment where I can freely and vibrantly engage like you do, morning and evening. That’s why you may not know how good the youth period is. You don’t realize how good it is. (laughter)  
However, after turning 30, getting married, having children, and becoming a responsible person after 40, you will realize how good this time is. You, who are so hopeful and have bright futures ahead of you wherever you go, have come into the Unification Church. (laughter, applause)  
Moreover, because America has a free spirit, educated people can go wherever they want, but when they come into the Unification Church, they find that there is only one path they must take, and you have thought a lot about your past, your environment, and your future path. Is that right? "Yes." Some people say, "Oh, in the Unification Church..." (laughter) and some people... (laughter) say they want to go, but their feet keep getting pulled back. I know very well that you are living that kind of life.  
So, how are your eyes? (mimicking, laughter) And your mouths are like this, and your feet are like that... (laughter) and my heart is everywhere. (laughter)  
Today, I want to see a show of hands from those who are meeting the teacher for the first time. Put your hands down. There may be people who came saying, "The teacher from the Unification Church is here, so let’s see what he looks like!" and "Let’s see how the teacher looks!" So, how do you feel after coming? (laughter, applause) I appreciate that you are applauding me.  
If I can give you freedom and liberation, or spiritual freedom and spiritual liberation, there is the fact that there are physical constraints and physical restrictions, which I see as contradictory. You all know that well. In that contradictory fact, we... Even if you don’t have a religion, you will feel it well in the general ethical world and in our lives.  
So, looking at it this way, those who do what their outer bodies want at first may feel good, but in the end, they will keep going down. However, those who do inner work may find it difficult at first but will keep rising. The paths diverge. Among these two paths, which path have we chosen? "The latter." That’s what we are. In fact, we are people who have chosen the inner world. We are of a different kind. You all must first understand that we are of a different kind than ordinary people.  
That’s why, from that perspective, there is no difference between me, the teacher, and you. We must walk the same path. So, what I want to talk about today is the common task we must undertake together as the teacher and you. Let’s talk with the title "Common Responsibility."  
Among the paths that humans must take, the hardest and most difficult path is...  
Now, you may be curious about when I started walking this path. To describe my character, I am a strong person, and there is nothing I cannot do. I am a capable person. I am good at sports; I can do everything in athletics. In terms of strength, I am not inferior to anyone, and in every aspect, I am not inferior to anyone. I also have brilliant ideas and strong thoughts. (laughter)  
That’s why, when I look back at my childhood, I was a person who could not sleep without knowing what was around me, what was visible. I was someone who did not know how to rest. I was someone who had a lot of interest in what insects lived there, what fish were there, what animals and birds were there, and how the valleys and mountains were formed. I was someone who could not sleep without knowing all that.  
So, when I do something, once I start, I don’t know how to stop for 24 hours. I forget to eat, and I forget whether it’s day or night. Sometimes, I forget whether it’s evening or morning. When I quickly look, evening looks like morning. So, when I decide to do something, I have stayed up all night.  
Even when I look at myself, I don’t think I’m stupid, and I believe that if I had studied, I would have become a world-renowned scholar. Since I have such a mind, I seriously thought about what I would do if I became a scholar. Wouldn’t I just end up studying all my life, hunched over at the blackboard, eating chalk dust? **Era’s Blessing**

This morning, I will speak on the topic of "Era’s Blessing." You have learned through the Principle that all spirits in the spirit world cannot enter the ideal heaven without receiving blessings through people on earth. Those in the spirit world are past people, while those living in the present are contemporary people. This current era connects the past, present, and future.

Heaven (the ideal world) is the world of love where God and family become one. Where is heaven realized? It is realized on earth. Where is perfection realized? It is realized on earth. Where is the perfection of God’s love realized? It is realized on earth. Now, when we think about the word "perfection," as you know, a man does not become perfect alone. A man and a woman must come together, but even just a man and a woman cannot achieve it. Here, God must be involved for it to be completed.

So where is ideal love realized? It cannot be just God alone. God cannot love alone. It cannot be just a man or just a woman. This threefold love must be completely united for eternal and unchanging ideal love to emerge, which you have learned in the Principle.

The decisive foundation that God desires is this earth, and what kind of place on this earth? It is a family formed by the union of a man and a woman centered on God’s love. That’s why when you think of "heaven," what concept should you have? You must always have the concept that heaven is the union of God, you, and your family. Even if you go to heaven, if God is not there, it cannot be heaven. God must be present. Can it be just God alone? Without your ideal partner, even God’s love is unnecessary for me. That’s why when you go to the spirit world, those who have lived an ideal couple life in this world are closer to God. This is an undeniable fact.

Where do you want to go? If you ask anyone, "Where do you want to go?" they will immediately say, "I want to go to the ideal world." So what is the ideal world? It is an unchanging and eternal world. It must also be absolute. That’s how it is.

However, no matter how unchanging, eternal, and absolute it is, if there is no love there, if there is no unchanging, eternal, and absolute love, it cannot be called an ideal. No one would say, "Ah, that world is the golden world because there is a lot of gold!" If that were the case, people who love gold would all claim it as their own, and fights would break out. If the whole heaven were a golden plate, everyone would say, "That’s mine, this is mine, all of this is mine." They would all be like that. If it goes on endlessly, they cannot reach the end, and standing in such a place, they would say, "That’s all mine!" Would that be heaven?

If heaven is a world of knowledge where "Ah, that world is good because you can know everything!" then they would look into each other and evaluate who is high and who is low. How complicated would that world be? Have you seen scholars? They assert their claims, become enemies with each other, and absolutely do not communicate... This cannot be heaven. If there is power there... if it is a world where power asserts itself, that would be a big problem. All of that cannot be essential conditions for heaven. The only thing that can be is that world must be a world of love, and we can conclude this. This is the ideal conclusion. Do you think so? "Yes."

Is parental love more fundamental than conjugal love? That love that changes in the morning, changes in the evening, and changes all year round? "No. Unchanging love..." Unchanging love has no beginning and no end. It goes on endlessly. For that love to be endless, must it go straight or turn? "It must turn." Why? When a man and a woman love, it is straight, but it can be straight as much as it wants... (Laughter) The reason it must turn is that if there are just the spouses, there must be parents, and also God, and sons and daughters must all be there. Only then can everything connect.
If you draw a line, would this line and that line all be different? If it's a circle, they are all the same. But if you go like this... the force that was going this way cannot go like this. It is obstructed in its path. However, at the same time, it can go in any direction without hindering the formation. Once you enter a room, everything is the same... 

In terms of electricity, it flows easily where it can. Now, if there is resistance here, the electricity won't flow this way. But if everything is the same, it means it can go anywhere without issue. What is resistance? It means "don't come." The absence of resistance means "come." It draws you in. This is the same principle.

From this perspective, the love between husband and wife should revolve around God's love, God's love should revolve around parental love, and parental love should revolve around children's love. I've seen couples fighting, saying, "Why don't you love me?" and fighting over love, but have you ever seen couples sitting together and saying, "Why do you love our children?" Ultimately, they might argue, "Why don't you love our children?" but there is no fight over love. That can happen. Have you ever seen parents fighting over loving their children? Have you ever seen mom and dad fighting because they love their children? "No, we haven't." They fight over not loving, but they say to love the children instead. They prefer to love beyond themselves and dislike not loving.

That is the center, and we can discover that here. Why? Because in the love between spouses, there are fights over not loving, but in the love for children, there are fights over the need to love. It's different. Why is that better? Because it follows the way closer to heavenly law.

When we question whether God's will has been fulfilled in today's world or in this universe, we know that it has not been fulfilled. This is because our human ancestors fell and fell into a position unrelated to God's will. 

From this perspective, it is an undeniable fact that while there is a path that God's original will follows and a world that His will aims for, there is also a path for fallen humanity to find that will again. 

There is a will that individuals must follow, as well as a will that families must follow, and then there is a will that transcends tribes and must be followed by nations, and there is a will that the world must follow. It is certain that God had an ideal of creation in which there is a world that people should follow, so no matter how much humanity has fallen and how evil the human world may be, we must understand that the path of that will still remains. God is absolute, eternal, unchanging, and unique, so His will must also be absolute, eternal, unchanging, and unique.

Through the history of fallen humanity, we learn through principles that God has taken on the responsibility to lift these fallen humans back to their original position through the providence of restoration for salvation, even if it requires personal, familial, national, and global sacrifices. However, it is a fact that the world cannot bend God's will to fit human desires, no matter how much sacrifice is made. 

God, who bears the responsibility to bring these fallen humans back to their original will, has been promoting the providence of restoration for the purpose of returning this fallen human world to its original state.

Isn’t that right? “Yes.” From now on, you need to evangelize at least twelve people. This is where you start to rise to the seventy. This is the restoration, this is the growth, and this is the completion. (Speaking while writing on the board) Why does it change within a year? It’s because, centered on last year, the time has changed according to the teacher's words. 
Now, as I mentioned earlier, a way has been opened to connect everything with heaven, so there is no hindrance for you on your path. It’s easy, you see? Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” Until now, it was not the time to evangelize your own mother, father, or siblings. Why is that? Because God sacrificed His sons and daughters to save the children of the enemy, Cain, as part of the restoration providence. Therefore, to evangelize your direct lineage, to evangelize your parents and siblings, is the same as evangelizing God, the same as evangelizing Jesus. So, when it comes to Jesus, He must ultimately overcome Rome and return. He must overcome the world and return. You must start from here at home, pass through Rome, and return to your nation. (Speaking while writing on the board) 
From the current perspective, if Korea is like Israel, then America is like Rome. Helping Korea is like what Rome did. In the time of Jesus, Judaism opposed Him, and in the time of the Unification Church, Christianity opposes us, just the same. Right now, Judaism and all government agencies are trying every possible means to eliminate the Unification Church and expel Reverend Moon, but it won’t go as they wish. Do you understand? Reverend Moon cannot be captured and killed. 
Just like when Jesus went to Rome and rebuked all the Romans, for three and a half years, the teacher has been playing this game in America. They all curse, saying America will perish. Jesus left His home to save the nation, didn’t He? To save the nation, He had to leave His home and go toward Rome. This is what you need to understand. Do you understand? “Yes.” Why was that? 
To save the great Cain first is to save the world quickly. 
Between the Eastern and Western opponents of Reverend Moon, which is the greater opponent? “The Western opponent is the greater opponent.” That’s right. If the central country, America, opposes, then all countries in the world will oppose as well. Why is that? Korea has suffered, and why did we leave that behind to come here? Why must it be so? Because God said so. Because America is the greater enemy, if we can quickly save the greater enemy, the smaller enemies will automatically be saved. Do you understand what I mean? 
Until now, history has been about striking God's direct lineage to save the enemy. That’s why Jesus also left His home. His own mother, father, and siblings were all enemies. They all mocked Jesus, saying, “If you want to reveal yourself, why are you sitting here? Go up to Jerusalem!” He had to fulfill his responsibility for his tribe, nation, and the world before He could return home. 
God has not been able to carry out such a history until now. It has begun in the era of Reverend Moon. I have left everything behind and come to America to lay the foundation for victory; now is the time to return. It is the time to establish Cain in the Abel position through victory and to entrust the heavenly work and return. 
Do you know why your parents oppose you? Do you know why your siblings oppose you? It is because of the law of heaven; it is God's strategy to make you keep the law of heaven. It is to set the condition that you loved the world more than your own mother, your own siblings, and your own relatives. Do you understand what I mean? This is wonderful. 
Do you know why your parents act that way? They unconsciously want to oppose you. That is to determine you as a person of heaven. Your parents may be in the satanic world, but after determining the kingdom of heaven, that person can return to your home and save you. 
Today, centered on the members of the Unification Church and Reverend Moon, we must achieve victory and return on the basis of individuals, families, nations, and the world. That’s why you must understand that I have invested my life and all my possessions into the American mission. Do you understand that? That’s why I laid the foundation in 1976. Now, I can leave America at any time. If I want to go, I can go; if I don’t want to go, I don’t have to. Do you understand what I mean? 
When I leave, I will sing praises and worship before God... I have no regrets about returning. I have fulfilled my mission. I am not saying that I will come back after ascending like Jesus, but when I leave here, I will not return; I will leave everything to you. 
From now on, when you return to your hometown and evangelize your family, 
if Korea is hell on earth, then America is heaven. However, there are people here who are on the side opposing heaven. If I lose, I will remain in the satanic world. However, through victory, I can manage America. Do you understand what I mean? It has come to that time. I have completed all the work in these three years, so now I can return... I can leave everything to you, and there is no threat to your lives. Even if you go out, there is no one who will try to kill you. 
The teacher has been under threat to life until now. I knew that an incident would occur during the Yankee Stadium event. That’s why heaven sent a storm to everyone... All those events happened because heaven loves us. The evil ones came first and then all left. You need to understand that many people with pistols came there. Do you understand? This is the fight we are engaged in. 
No matter how difficult it gets, no one thinks of trying to kill you. Why is that? Because heaven killed Abel whom it loved. To bear fruit from the history where Cain killed Abel, we must engage in such work as a global nation, and that is how it bears fruit. However, from the teacher's position, it cannot be done that way. Do you understand what I mean? So, the teacher has parents, many older brothers, and many relatives, but you must understand that until now, I have never spoken the Principle even once. 
Even though there are many relatives, it is God's work to love external people first and then find one’s own clan. 
Next, what does it mean that the time is different now? It means that the members of the Unification Church are also to follow this and return to their hometowns after working externally on a global scale. So, you must understand that it is now the time to evangelize your own mother and father and your siblings. 
You have suffered in the satanic world, feeling the sorrow of being a nationless, homeless, parentless, and siblingless person, but now you can honor your mother as your mother, your brother as your brother, and your relatives as your relatives, and you can accept your nation without opposition. When you realize that fact, a great event will unfold where you return home and become the emperor of your homeland, saving that nation. 
Now is the time to evangelize your family. Do you understand? By the 1980s, you will all be driven back home. Once the seven years of public life are over, you will all return home. Do you understand what I mean? Now, how easy is it for you to evangelize? It is tenfold or a hundredfold harder to evangelize the world. Because you are returning home to evangelize, no matter how much your family hates and persecutes you, they will not kill you. You must understand that. 
You only need to put in one-fifth of the effort you used to put in to evangelize one person outside. What do you think? “Wow! That person has changed so much... Has that person really changed?” If that happens, you can gather all your relatives and lecture them on the Principle, and within one hour, two hours, three hours, or seven hours, you can evangelize hundreds of people. Until now, why did we set the number at three people? It was to establish a direction. You had to evangelize three people to establish one direction to rise up. (Speaking while writing on the board) After you have reached this point, it is time to evangelize in all directions. Do you understand? 
When entering the kingdom of heaven, you enter through one door, but when living in the kingdom of heaven, you must go through the twelve pearl gates. Is that necessary or not? Therefore, it is time to have twelve people representing the twelve pearl gates. Jacob had twelve sons, didn’t he? The nation of Israel has twelve tribes, right? It is so in families, and then in clans, and then in nations. When viewed centered on Jesus, when forming a new Israel representing the twelve tribes of the nation of Israel, it starts with the twelve disciples on a super-national standard. Do you understand? “Yes.” 
So from now on, it is not the teacher who should take the lead; it is you who must take the lead. Do you understand? You must make America into heaven. What you have done, you will definitely reap. What the teacher has done until now is to distribute the seeds throughout the world. I have given you the seeds. Do I need to sow and weed it all myself? “No.” 
Now, you must return home and, centered on your home, deal with the twelve brothers... centered on Jacob's seventy-two disciples, and the one hundred twenty disciples, you must resolve everything within one household. To do that, you must surpass Jesus. Did Jesus create one disciple? “No.” You must do the work of creating one person from one hundred twenty nations. Do you understand? That’s why it is a global era. The one hundred twenty disciples of Jesus expanded to one hundred twenty nations. Therefore, if Reverend Moon does not go to even one of the one hundred twenty nations, the spirit world will accuse him, saying, “If you have the heavenly will and have the responsibility to save all people, why did you leave our nation out?” 
Did the teacher do all that or not? “He did it all.” Even to the satellite nations. You may not know, but the youth must understand that you must fight with the resolve to risk your lives. Should you move more than that when you go to New York, or not? “We must move.” It is that time. 
The time is different. The environment is different. The time has changed. Do you understand? Based on the foundation of victory in 1976, we are entering a new era centered on the birthday of the teacher in 1977. It is that time. So, by holding onto your mother and father and crying, your mother and father can be saved immediately. 
To restore parents, the condition of Cain and Abel becoming one must be established; otherwise, fallen Adam and Eve cannot be saved. Salvation can only be obtained through Abel, that is, through the children. To restore parents, it cannot be done with Abel alone. The condition that Abel and Cain have become one must be established for the parents to be restored. The younger brother must become the older brother, and the older brother must take the place of the younger brother to be restored. Isn’t that right? Originally, the firstborn is to be the heir, but if the firstborn stood in the blessing of heaven, this fallen world would not have happened. Because of the fall, Satan took the position of the firstborn, and heaven took the position of the secondborn. 
Now, look. America, which opposed Reverend Moon, has become a fortune that supports Reverend Moon. Because of that, from a global perspective, the teacher's family can resurrect and save all from parents to ancestors at once. Why is that? Because the son can save the parents, and then that son can save the parents... This means that everything can be restored. Therefore, since the entire spirit world is in a position connected to the parents’ position, the entire spirit world can descend to the earth and create heaven. Then, a great event will unfold in the spirit world. Do you understand? “Yes.” 
From a historical perspective, because Cain and Abel have become one and can restore parents centered on them, it has become a global origin for the restoration movement of parents, which can unfold flatly centered on the believers of the Unification Church. It is the same theory. Do you understand what I mean? 
If the parents, heaven, and the children can become one, then the whole world will be in their hands... They can command and everything. If a family is formed where Adam and Eve did not fall, there cannot be Satan. Concerning Satan, “Hey! The world is on my side, and the spirit world is on my side, so where do you think you can go?” can be said. Do you understand? The theory fits perfectly. All conditions for indemnity will be settled. 
Thus, the era of the providence of salvation, where the internal person was sacrificed for the external person, has passed, and it is the time when God can bless the earth when He rejoices centered on His sons and daughters, His bloodline. You must understand that the time has come when you can pair up those who were separated in the spirit world, such as your mother, father, grandparents, and everyone else, through you. Therefore, a new era of registration will unfold in both spirit and flesh. Do you understand? Such events will unfold. 
Such a tremendous and incredible event is happening, but you may not know it, do you? Do you know or not? The teacher is saying, “This year is a new year.” What is new? That’s why I am teaching you clearly. Because you have the foundation that the teacher has laid, you must realize that the time of reunion, where Adam, who was cast out by God, returns to God with joy, is approaching you, a time that cannot be met without tears. 
Our missionaries, too, by 1980, will all withdraw and return home. Do you understand? Until 1980, we have indemnity conditions remaining. The communist world remains. Therefore, we must lay the foundation and build it up over three years. Then, the communists will collapse massively. Just wait and see what happens. 
Recently, there has been famine in China, and this year there is famine in the Soviet Union; such events keep occurring, right? China is in chaos due to earthquakes. In contrast, the young people are explosively increasing. The second generation is on the teacher's side, right? Do you understand? That’s why all the second generation in America are coming here. This is the time that matches the global wilderness era, the wilderness era of the Israelite people heading toward the land of Canaan; if you oppose heaven, you will fall in the wilderness. Everything will perish. 
However, because you have encountered this global time, a time when you can save your perishing parents, you will not perish. Why is that? Because the time has come to return home after finishing all external work and to save your hometown, you will not perish. Do you understand? “Yes.” Everything is set up that way. That’s why we must go to the new era, the new era. Do you understand? “Yes.” 
Evangelize twelve people. 
So now, who will establish the tradition of this new era? You will establish it. From now on, you in America must take the lead until 1980. In the years 1978, 1979, and 1980, for three and a half years, you will be pushed to establish the tradition of America.
You must establish it. You need to understand that the tradition of serving the country and loving the world for three and a half years must be established through you.  
The hippies in America are all Cain hippies, and you are Abel hippies. What does it mean to be a hippie? All hippies are communist factions. What is a hippie? They are those who engage in free sex, have loose morals, and claim that there is no home, no mother and father, no nation, nothing at all. Abel hippies, on the other hand, focus on family, the nation, and the world... Furthermore, Abel hippies are all about fighting against communism... it's the opposite, right?  
If we do this for just three years, the hippies will completely unite with the Unification Church externally. On that day, you will all return home and bring your grandparents back together... thus restoring your parents. That is the principle, right? Isn't it? "Yes." That is the principle, and today's era is exactly like that.  
What kind of blood do you have? "Abel hippie, hippie." What about over there? "Cain hippie, hippie." Over there, men and women are promiscuous, but here it is strict. It's the opposite. They are dazed and wasting time, while we are working hard to the point of our eyes popping out and our bones breaking. Can our Unification Church members date? "No." Then what are we doing? What are we doing? We are finding families, finding nations, finding the world, and within that, we must marry in a place where the world welcomes us, the nation welcomes us, and the family welcomes us. I have already prepared that internal environment. If you say, "Teacher, that's good. That's good," it means you want to take everything the teacher has prepared for free.  
So, why do we do hard things? Why do we do hard things? We do the hardest things all at once... then we can share everything at once. If you do this much and then that much, how will you survive? Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." If I just sign, that signature will apply to a thousand people, ten thousand people, all the same. A thousand people can participate together. A thousand people can act with the same effectiveness.  
Now that the three-year period is over, you in America have worked hard, so I must distribute all the gifts... That is why I have set a special period of 40 days. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." The time... until now, I have brought money and used it, but now you must earn the money I will use. Until America reaches this point, I have covered all the expenses for three years, but now you must earn the money for me to live and use. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."  
To do this, you must go to the front line. The front line where the teacher fought is my front line! If I make you greedy, it will fall under the condition of indemnity, making you all regret and feel wronged, but now if you fight, everything will become yours. There is no indemnity. It will become yours. Is that a curse or a blessing? "A blessing."  
You must witness to twelve people. So starting today, do not rest and write letters to twelve people. Do not take a day off; write letters to everyone you can, including older brothers, sisters, and distant relatives. Especially those who are out and about, those who are fundraising, just a few lines on cards or picture postcards will do. You can all do it. If you do this, it won't take three years. You can do it all within a year. Do you understand what I mean? How many people do you need to witness to? "Twelve people." Why? Because I need twelve people to be the center. If you think of the four directions and four seasons, three months each centered around twelve (3×4=12), it becomes twelve months, and in the spirit world, there are twelve pearl gates, so we must witness to twelve people who can guard the representative gates that can pass through the twelve pearl gates.  
Will there be disciples who will sell out Jesus there? Do you think they will sell out their older brothers, younger brothers, sons, or nephews? "No." Why? Because they are older brothers, sisters, younger brothers, fathers, uncles, and cousins. Who will sell them out? In that sense, you are better than Jesus. You must understand that having a family-oriented environment makes you better than Jesus. You must also understand that being able to have a family without going outside is better. Furthermore, you stand in a position where you can pave the way without fulfilling the conditions of indemnity, so you must understand that you are better than Jesus.  
Just as there are twelve pearl gates in the heavenly kingdom, there must also be twelve gates on earth. That is resurrection. Then, there are 72 elders, 120 disciples, and this must be done within three years... The teacher, centered around twelve families and twelve disciples, will combine this into 36 families, then 72 families, then 120 families, then 430 families, then 777 families, and then 1,800 families... This refers to the Old Testament, New Testament, and Completed Testament eras. This refers to the families of Adam, Noah, and Jacob. Do you understand? I have married them all off. I have sent them all to get married. Do you understand? Even if you can't marry them off, you must do all this, right? Even if you can't marry them off, you must at least create one group, right?  
Let's cross the watershed.  
If you are one step better than me, I have done this with external people, but you can do it with your own family. That is better than me. How envious I must be of that. If I had said this to my parents, to my beloved older brothers and sisters, they would have said, "Oh, my younger sibling! Oh, my children! Don't suffer..." and would have done all sorts of things for me, but I have done this work while being persecuted and abandoned. I have done this work throughout my life while being opposed and chased. Just like Cain killed Abel, they are trying to kill me. I have always been crossing the line between life and death while doing this work.  
Now, do you understand the time? Do you know what kind of time it is? "Yes." It is a time when you can carry on the teacher's work even without the teacher. Do you understand? "Yes." From now on, you are entering a time when you can do this for three and a half years. The same principles apply to Unification Church members in America and around the world.  
Once the Unification Church members fulfill their responsibilities, the teacher will truly be free. Isn't that right? After that, whether I go anywhere in the world with a cane, I will be well taken care of. There are many blessed families in the world, so wherever I go, I will be treated better than the king of that country. (Applause) The clans will all join in and do this work together. The clans will unite and consider it a great honor to serve the teacher, saying, "Oh! Please come once." That will happen. In the future, it won't just be round-trip expenses; they will spend all costs to invite me. If airplane tickets come in, I will distribute them to each of you. It will definitely happen. Do you think it will happen or not? "I think it will." So, which families will I visit first? I will first go to the homes of those who have had international marriages. Do you understand what I mean?  
The teacher is someone who has made a heart-centered revolution. Do you have any objections to that? Yes or no? "No." That is why you understand about these 40 days, right? What is this watershed? What did I say earlier? What is the spelling? Watershed? Do you understand what that means? You must cross this. Once you cross it, you will not come back again. Do you understand? That is why I have spoken for over six hours today, past twelve o'clock, because you must understand it clearly.  
That is why you must understand that the time has changed. From now on, you must boast about it. You must boast. "Mun is really good. Better than any prince of any country, better than any president's son." You must boast like that. You must prepare for about three years from now to boast about the world. Do you think that will happen or not? "I will do it." I hope you will pass through this 40-day period well. It took me 40 years. You must indemnify this in 40 days. Will that happen or not? "It will!"*
